	function display_endemol_app ()
	{

		var flashvars = {
		  containerName: "endemol_app",
		  dataURI: "http://sports.williamhill.com/bir_xml",
		  streamDataURI: "http://sports.williamhill.com/bet/en-gb",
		  performAccessKeyURI:    "",
		  performAntiLeachingURI: "",
		  unastvStreamURI: "",
		  userID: "",
		  priceFormat: "",
		  allBetLive: "",
		  //myBetLive: "false",
		  classID:"",
		  typeID: "",
		  categoryID:"",
		  eventID: "",
		  staticContent: document.endemol_url + "/bir_images",
		  categoryExceptions: "1,2,13,20,16",
		  HTTPFailureMessage: "Sorry, we cannot access the data at the moment.",
		  reducedMode: ""
		};

		var params = {allowScriptAccess: "always", WMODE: "opaque" };
		var attributes = {allowScriptAccess: "always"};

		if (document.getElementById("endemol_app") == null) {
			// QC6076: swfobject doesn't check to see if endemol_app actually exists
			// if it doesn't, it just breaks and errors.
		} else if (DetectFlashVer("9","0","0")) {
			removeClass(document.getElementById("endemol_app"), "displayNone");
			addClass(document.getElementById("alternative_to_flash"), "displayNone");
			addClass(document.getElementById("download_flash_link"), "displayNone");
			swfobject.embedSWF(document.endemol_url + "/WilliamHill.swf" + "?ver=86da42e8ca52528ce2660fd0b2e666af", "endemol_app", "646", "50", "9.0.0", document.endemol_url + "/expressInstall.swf" + "?ver=86da42e8ca52528ce2660fd0b2e666af", flashvars, params, attributes );
		} else if (DetectFlashVer("6", "0", "65")) {
			//we have between flash 6.0.65 and 9.0.0
			removeClass(document.getElementById("endemol_app"), "displayNone");
			removeClass(document.getElementById("alternative_to_flash"), "displayNone");
			addClass(document.getElementById("download_flash_link"), "displayNone");
				//move the alternative content to above the upgrade flash div
			document.getElementById("download_flash_link").parentNode.insertBefore
				(document.getElementById("endemol_app"), document.getElementById("download_flash_link"));
			swfobject.embedSWF(document.endemol_url + "/WilliamHill.swf" + "?ver=86da42e8ca52528ce2660fd0b2e666af", "endemol_app", "665", "50%", "9.0.0", document.endemol_url + "/expressInstall.swf" + "?ver=86da42e8ca52528ce2660fd0b2e666af", flashvars, params, attributes );
		} else {
			addClass(document.getElementById("endemol_app"), "displayNone");
			removeClass(document.getElementById("alternative_to_flash"), "displayNone");
			removeClass(document.getElementById("download_flash_link"), "displayNone");
		}
	}

	//Allowing the endemol flash betting in running application
	// to change the height of it's div
	function setDivHeight( h ){

		// First hide the loading image if it is present
		var loadingDiv = document.getElementById ( "endemol_loading" );

		if (loadingDiv != null &amp;&amp; loadingDiv.style.visibility != "hidden") {
			loadingDiv.style.visibility = "hidden";
			// Hidden divs tend to make white space, so lets take care of that
			loadingDiv.height = 0;
			loadingDiv.width = 0;
		}

		var div = document.getElementById( "endemol_app" );
		div.style.height = h + "px";
	}

function readCookie( cName ){
  var v;
  return decodeURIComponent( ( v = ( document.cookie || "" ).match( "(^|\\s)" + cName + "=([^;]+)" ) ) ? v[ 2 ] : "" );
}
</script>

<script>
function trafalgarOptOut() {
  if (setCookie &amp;&amp; document.pref_cookie_path &amp;&amp; document.pref_cookie_domain) {
    var expiryDate = new Date('January 01, 2000');
    setCookie('wh_traf_public_beta', 'No', expiryDate, document.pref_cookie_path, document.pref_cookie_domain, ''); 
    setCookie('sitePreference', '', expiryDate, document.pref_cookie_path, document.pref_cookie_domain, ''); 
    setCookie('mbox', '', expiryDate, document.pref_cookie_path, document.pref_cookie_domain, ''); 
    window.location.reload();
  }
}

if ((typeof jQuery !== "undefined") &amp;&amp; (window.location.pathname.indexOf('/betting') === 0) &amp;&amp;
(jQuery('.header__inner').is(':visible')) &amp;&amp;
(readCookie("wh_traf_reg_completed") !== "true") &amp;&amp;
(readCookie("wh_traf_public_beta") !== "mobet")) {
  jQuery(document).ready(function() {
    var greenBar = document.createElement("div");
    greenBar.className = "green_bar";
    var greenBarWrapElement = document.createElement("div");
    greenBarWrapElement.className = "wrap";
    var greenBarLink = document.createElement("a");
    greenBarLink.setAttribute("title", "Go Back");
    greenBarLink.innerHTML = "Want to return to our existing site? Click here";
    greenBarLink.href = "javascript:trafalgarOptOut();";
    greenBarWrapElement.appendChild(greenBarLink);
    greenBar.appendChild(greenBarWrapElement);
    document.body.insertBefore(greenBar, document.body.childNodes[0]);
  });
}
</script>

	document.depositStarted_EPYV = "false";
	document.depositStarted_IKSH = "false";
	document.depositStarted_MB = "false";
	document.depositStarted_NTLR = "false";
	document.depositStarted_PPAL = "false";
	document.depositStarted_PSC = "false";
	document.depositStarted_UKSH = "false";

	$(document).ready(function() {
		$('.joinNowLink').click(function() {
			return showRegModal(
				'https://sports.williamhill.com/acc/en-gb/register/SB/register.html',
				null,
				document.site.regModal.width,
				document.site.regModal.height
			);
		});

		$('a#close, a#backToSiteBtn').click(function(e) {
			// Google Analytics tracking
			trackCloseOrContinueContinuePlaying(this.id);

			try {
				e.preventDefault();
				// If window.opener exists, this is a popup.
				var handler = window.opener ? window.opener : window.parent;
				// Call postmessage handler to close the overlay
				handler.postMessage("modal_close", "*");
			} catch(err) {
				// if postMessage is not supported (eg IE7), use basic alternative:
				window.location = 'http://sports.williamhill.com/bet/en-gb?action=GoModalClose';
			}
		});

		$('a#goUpdateAcct').click(function(e) {
			try {
				e.preventDefault();
				// Call postmessage handler to close the overlay
				 window.parent.postMessage("modal_close_and_update_acct", "*");
			} catch(err) {
				// if postMessage is not supported (eg IE7), use basic alternative:
				window.location = '?action=GoAcctUpdate';
			}
		});

		$('a#goSpainNoId').click(function(e) {
			try {
				e.preventDefault();
				// Call postmessage handler to close the overlay
				window.parent.postMessage("modal_close_and_show_verification", "*");
			} catch(err) {
				// if postMessage is not supported (eg IE7), use basic alternative
				window.location = '?action=GoVerification';
			}
		});

		

	});

	function loadDefaultPage() {
		var cgi_url = "http://sports.williamhill.com/bet/en-gb";
		var new_cgi_url = cgi_url.substring(0, cgi_url.indexOf("?"));
		window.location.href = cgi_url;
		return;
	}

	function receiveMessage(event)
	{
		if (event.data == "modal_close") {
			//Remove GN redirect parameter from URL when closed
			if (window.location.href.indexOf("GNRegRedirect") != -1) {
				var close_url = window.location.href.replace("/GNRegRedirect", "");
				window.location.href = close_url;
				return;
			}

			
			if (window.location.href == "https://sports.williamhill.com/acc/en-gb/register/SB/aff_register.html" ||
				window.location.href.indexOf("payment/deposit/modal_deposit.html") != -1 ||
				window.location.href.indexOf("action=GoDeposit") != -1) {
					window.location.href = "http://sports.williamhill.com/bet/en-gb";
					return;
				}

			
			if (getUrlVars(window.location.href)["action"] == "DoWithdrawConfirm") {
				window.location.href = "https://sports.williamhill.com/acc/en-gb?action=GoAcct";
			} else {
				var retry = 0 ;
				
				if ((window.location.href.indexOf("showResub") !=-1) || (retry == 1) ) {
					loadDefaultPage();
					return;
				}

				window.location.reload();
			}
		} else if (event.data == "modal_close_and_update_acct") {
			window.location.href = "?action=GoAcctUpdate";
		} else if (event.data == "modal_close_and_show_verification") {
			window.location.href = "?action=GoVerification";
		}
	}

	if (window.addEventListener) {  // Non IE browsers
		window.addEventListener ("message", receiveMessage, false);
	}
	else if (window.attachEvent) {   // IE browsers
		window.attachEvent("onmessage", receiveMessage);
	}

	function getUrlVars(url) {
		var vars = {};
		var parts = url.replace(/[?&amp;]+([^=&amp;]+)=([^&amp;]*)/gi, function(m,key,value) {
			vars[key] = value;
		});
		return vars;
	}

	function showRegModal(action,target,width,height) {
		//Parameter sanitization

		//Parameter action is mandatory
		if (typeof action == 'undefined' || action == null || action == "") {
			return;
		}

		if (typeof target == 'undefined') {
			target = null;
		}

		if (typeof width  == 'undefined') {
			width = document.site.regModal.width;
		}

		if (width == null || width == "" || width &lt; 0 ) {
			return;
		}

		if (typeof height == 'undefined') {
			height = document.site.regModal.height;
		}

		if (height == null || height == "" || height &lt; 0 ) {
			return;
		}

		_showRegModal(action,target,width,height);
	}

	function _showRegModal(action,target,width,height) {
		// Customer is logged in so must be redirected to accounts page
		
		
		// By default the enable scrolling var is set to false
		var regOverlayScrolling = false;
		
		

		if (typeof action == 'undefined') {
			// Invalid action specified. Don't show overlay.
			return;
		}

		var overlayClass = 'regModal';
		// switch class for IE7

		if ($.browser.msie &amp;&amp; parseInt($.browser.version, 10) == 7) {
			overlayClass = 'regModalIe7';
		}

		document.site.regModalOverlay = new Overlay(action, width, height, overlayClass, false, false, "regModalFrame", '', '', true,false,false,regOverlayScrolling);

		if ( document.site.regModalOverlay.init() ) {
			document.site.regModalOverlay.show();
			getObject(document.site.regModalOverlay.frame_id).focus();
		}

		if (typeof target != 'undefined') {
			document.site.regModalTarget = target;
		} else {
			document.site.regModalTarget = null;
		}

		// Google Analytics tracking
		if (action.indexOf("register") != -1) {
			document.GARegistration.SendRegistrationTrack("Open");
		}

		$("#overlayFunc").css('display', 'block');
		return false;
	}

	// Google Analytics tracking helper function
	function gaStartRegistrationTracking(track_form_name) {
		if (document.registrationStarted == "false") {
			startTimer(track_form_name);
			document.GARegistration.SendRegistrationTrack("Start");
			document.GAForms.SendFormsTrack(track_form_name,"Start");
			document.registrationStarted = "true";
		}
	}

	// Google Analytics tracking helper function
	function gaStartDepositTracking(form_name, track_mthd) {
		if (document.depositStarted == "false") {
			startTimer(form_name);
			form_name = (document.isCompleteReg == "true") ? "CompleteReg" : "Deposit";
			document.GAForms.SendFormsTrack(form_name,"Start");
			document.GADeposit.SendDepositTrack("Start");
			document.depositStarted = "true";
		}

		var mthd_started = document["depositStarted_" + track_mthd];
		if (mthd_started == "false") {
			document["depositStarted_" + track_mthd] = true;
			document.GAPaymethod.SendPaymethodTrack("Start", track_mthd);
		}
	}

	// Google Analytics tracking helper function to start tracking how long a user spends completing a form
	function startTimer(form_name) {
		var start_date = new Date();
		var start_time = start_date.getTime();

		if (form_name == "Reg") {
			document.registrationStartTime = start_time;
		} else {
			document.depositStartTime = start_time;
		}
	}

	// Google Analytics tracking helper function
	function sendFormsTracking(form_name, action) {
		var interval = calculateIntervalSeconds(form_name);
		if (form_name == "Deposit") {
			if (document.isCompleteReg == "true") {
				form_name = "CompleteReg";
			}
		}
		document.GAForms.SendFormsTrack(form_name, action, interval);
	}

	// Google Analytics tracking helper function to calculate how long a user has spent completing a form
	function calculateIntervalSeconds(form_name) {
		var end_date = new Date();
		var end_time = end_date.getTime();
		if (form_name == "Reg") {
			var start_time = document.registrationStartTime;
		} else {
			var start_time = document.depositStartTime;
		}

		if (start_time == null || start_time == "") {
			return "N/A";
		} else {
			var milliseconds_elapsed = end_time - start_time;
			var seconds_elapsed = parseInt(milliseconds_elapsed / 1000);
			return seconds_elapsed;
		}
	}

	// Google Analytics tracking helper function
	function sendConditionsPoliciesTracking(action) {
		if (action == "optinout") {
			if ($("#acceptTerms").attr('checked') == "checked") {
				document.GAConditionsPolicies.SendPolicyTracking('optin');
			} else {
				document.GAConditionsPolicies.SendPolicyTracking('optout');
			}
		} else {
			document.GAConditionsPolicies.SendPolicyTracking(action);
		}
	}

	// Google Analytics tracking helper function
	function sendPromosubscribeTracking(checkbox_name,action) {
		if ($("#" + checkbox_name).attr('checked') == "checked") {
			document.GAPromosubscribe.SendPromosubscribeTracking('optin');
		} else {
			document.GAPromosubscribe.SendPromosubscribeTracking('optout');
		}
	}

	function trackCloseOrContinueContinuePlaying(action) {
		if (action == "backToSiteBtn") {
			document.GADepSuccessForm.SendDepSuccessFormTrack('ContinuePlaying');
		} else {
			var current_form = setFormForTracking();
			document.GAForms.SendFormsTrack(current_form,'Close','');
		}
	}

	// Helper function for setting form name for Google Analytics form fields tracking
	function setFormForTracking() {
		if (document.isCompleteReg == "true") {
			var track_form_name = "CompleteReg";
		}
		else if (document.isCompleteReg == "false") {
			var track_form_name = "Deposit";
		}
		 else if (document.isDepositSuccess == "true") {
			var track_form_name = "Depositsuccess";
		} else {
			var track_form_name = "Reg";
		}
		return track_form_name;
	}

	// Following functions are added as wrappers to allow Canvases and Translations to call the 
	// Google Analytics functionality

	function sendCallUsTracking() {
		var track_form = setFormForTracking();
		document.GAHelp.SendHelpTracking('CallUs',track_form);
	}

	function sendEmailUsTracking() {
		var track_form = setFormForTracking();
		document.GAHelp.SendHelpTracking('Email',track_form);
	}

	function sendLiveChatTracking() {
		var track_form = setFormForTracking();
		document.GAHelp.SendHelpTracking('LiveChat',track_form);
	}

	function trackEmailDetails() {
		document.GADepSuccessForm.SendDepSuccessFormTrack('EmailDetails');
	}

	function trackPrintScreen() {
		document.GADepSuccessForm.SendDepSuccessFormTrack('PrintScreen');
	}

	function trackDepositAfterDeposit() {
		document.GADepSuccessForm.SendDepSuccessFormTrack('EmailDetails');
	}

	function trackTransferFunds() {
		document.GADepSuccessForm.SendDepSuccessFormTrack('TransferFunds');
	}

	function trackFreeBetsAndBonuses() {
		document.GADepSuccessForm.SendDepSuccessFormTrack('FreeBetsAndBonuses');
	}

	function trackAcctDetails() {
		document.GADepSuccessForm.SendDepSuccessFormTrack('AcctDetails');
	}

	function trackLostLoginRetrieve() {
		document.GALostLogin.SendLostLoginTracking();
	}

	// End of wrapper functions for Canvases and Translations

}

<script type="text/javascript">
	document.changePwdBox = function()
	{
		//if displayNone is not already a class elemtent
		var _tmp_pwd_div = getObject('tmp_pwd_div'),
			_pwd_div     = getObject('pwd_div'),
			_password    = getObject('password');

		if (!_tmp_pwd_div) return;

		if (getObject('tmp_pwd_div').className.indexOf('displayNone') == -1)
		{
			addClass('tmp_pwd_div', 'displayNone');
			removeClass('pwd_div', 'displayNone');
			getObject('password').focus();
		} else if (getObject('password').value == '') {
			addClass('pwd_div', 'displayNone');
			removeClass('tmp_pwd_div', 'displayNone');
		}
	}

	document.changeUsernameBox = function()
	{
		//if displayNone is not already a class elemtent
		var _tmp_username_div     = getObject('tmp_username_div'),
			_username_div     = getObject('username_div'),
			_username         = getObject('username');

		if (!_tmp_username_div) return;

		if (getObject('tmp_username_div').className.indexOf('displayNone') == -1)
		{
			addClass('tmp_username_div', 'displayNone');
			removeClass('username_div', 'displayNone');
			getObject('username').focus();
		} else if (getObject('username').value == '') {
			addClass('username_div', 'displayNone');
			removeClass('tmp_username_div', 'displayNone');
		}
	}

	
	document.setLocale = function(l,t) {

		// Show Not allowed message for Restricted Locales
		
			if (l == "it") {
				showPopUp("&lt;span class='popupTitle'&gt;Williamhill.it&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;William Hill ha creato un sito internet appositamente per l'Italia. Per i residenti in Italia  necessario procedere alla registrazione su tale sito. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Vai a &lt;a href='http://www.williamhill.it' target='_blank'&gt;www.williamhill.it&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;",null,null);

				return;
			}
		
			if (l == "es") {
				showPopUp("&lt;span class='popupTitle'&gt;Williamhill.es&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To comply with Spanish gaming regulations, William Hill has created a website specifically for Spanish residents.  If you are located in Spain, you must register on the regulated site. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Go to &lt;a href='http://sports.williamhill.es/'target='_blank'&gt;www.williamhill.es&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;",null,null);

				return;
			}
		

		document.site.set_locale(l,t);
	}

	function copyBlackBox(formId) {
		if (getObject("iovation")) {

		} else if (document.forms["iovation"]) {

		}
	}

function maxiGame(gameType, miniType) {
		if (!gameType || gameType=="") {gameType="Bingo";}
		if (!miniType) {miniType="";}
		var region = '';
		var strLangUp = 'EN';
		var strLang = strLangUp.toLowerCase();
		if (strLang == 'ie') {
			strLang = 'en';
			region = '&amp;region=Ireland';	
		}
		if (miniType == 'Cash Bingo') {
			miniType = 'Main';
		}
		if((miniType != undefined) &amp;&amp; (miniType != 'undefined') &amp;&amp; (miniType != '')) {
			bingo_window = window.open("https://sports.williamhill.com/bet/"+strLang+"?action=DoGameLaunch&amp;systemName=VirtueFusion&amp;base_url=https://williamhill.virtuefusion.com/igames/play/game_page.do&amp;lang=" +strLang + "&amp;source=BN&amp;miniGameType="+ miniType + region +"&amp;gameType=Bingo&amp;gameCode=BN" +strLangUp,"miniGame", "toolbar=no,width=800,height=550,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes");
			bingo_window.focus();
		}
		else {
			if(gameType == 'B5' || gameType == 'L5' || gameType == 'C5' || gameType == 'A5' || gameType == 'D5' || gameType == 'R5' || gameType == 'F5' || gameType == 'T5' || gameType == 'J5' || gameType == 'M5' || gameType == 'S5') {
				switch(strLang){
					case 'el': langLong = 'Greek'; break;
					case 'en': langLong = 'English'; break;
					case 'es': langLong = 'Spanish'; break;
					case 'fr': langLong = 'French'; break;
					case 'zh': langLong = 'Chinese'; break;
					case 'de': langLong = 'German'; break;
					case 'tr': langLong = 'Turkish'; break;
					case 'it': langLong = 'Italian'; break;
					case 'sv': langLong = 'Swedish'; break;
				} 
				switch(gameType){
					case 'A5': gamePath = '/AlicesWonderlandPPP_bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp; break;
					case 'B5': gamePath = '/3DRouletteppp_bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp+'&amp;'; break;

					case 'D5': gamePath = '/AroundTheWorld_Bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp+'&amp;'; break;
					case 'F5': gamePath = '/FruitMadness_Bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp+'&amp;'; break;
					case 'J5': gamePath = '/JewelsOfAtlantis_Bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp+'&amp;'; break;
					case 'L5': gamePath = '/LeprechaunsLuckSlotPPP_bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp+'&amp;'; break;
					case 'M5': gamePath = '/MidasMillions_Bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp+'&amp;'; break;
					case 'R5': gamePath = '/ReelGems_Bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp+'&amp;'; break;
					case 'S5': gamePath = '/Slotris_Bingo/game_load.asp&amp;gameCode='+gameType+strLangUp+'&amp;'; break;

	<div style="display: block; display: none;" id="modalDimmer"></div>
<div style="display: block; position: absolute; display: none;" id="modalPopup2">
	<div class="top" id="popupTop"></div>
	<div class="main" id="popupMain">
	<div>
		<p id="popText"></p>

		<div class="buttons">
			<a class="popupBtn linkable" id="yesBtn" onclick="javascript:hidePopUp(1);"><span>Yes</span></a>
			<a class="popupBtn linkable" id="noBtn" onclick="javascript:hidePopUp(0);"><span>No</span></a>
			<a class="popupBtn linkable" id="cancelBtn" onclick="javascript:hidePopUp(-1);"><span>Cancel</span></a>
		</div>

	<div class="clearboth"></div>

<script type="text/javascript">

var isInetExpSix = 0;

// popUpCallback function
var popUpCallBack = null;

// Extra jQuery fn for centering a selected object on the screen
jQuery.fn.center = function () {
    this.css("position","absolute");
    this.css("top", ( $(window).height() - this.height() ) / 2+$(window).scrollTop() + "px");
    this.css("left", ( $(window).width() - this.width() ) / 2+$(window).scrollLeft() + "px");
    return this;
}

// Reset the buttons to the default setup (all displayed)
function resetBtns () {
	$('.popupBtn').show();
}

// Set up the buttons for a yes / no prompt
function setupYesNo () {
	resetBtns();

	$('#cancelBtn').hide();

	$('#yesBtn').html('Yes');
	$('#noBtn').html('No');

}

// Set up a just OK dialog
function setupOK (buttontext) {
	resetBtns();

	$('#noBtn').hide();
	$('#cancelBtn').hide();

	if (buttontext == null || buttontext == undefined) {
		$('#yesBtn').html('OK');
	} else {
		$('#yesBtn').html(buttontext);
	}
}

// Set up a OK dialog with cancel button
function setupOKCancel (buttontext) {
	resetBtns();

	$('#noBtn').hide();

	if (buttontext == null || buttontext == undefined) {
		$('#yesBtn').html('OK');
	} else {
		$('#yesBtn').html(buttontext);
	}
}

function setupNoBtn () {
	resetBtns();

	$('#yesBtn').hide();
	$('#noBtn').hide();
	$('#cancelBtn').hide();

}

// Set up a yes / no / cancel dialog
function setupYesNoCancel () {
	resetBtns();

	$('#yesBtn').html('Yes');
	$('#noBtn').html('No');
	$('#cancelBtn').html('Cancel');
}

// Hide the pop up box
function hidePopUp (response) {

	if (popUpCallBack != null) {
		var funcCall = popUpCallBack + "(" + response + ");";
		var ret = eval(funcCall);
	}

	if (isInetExpSix) {
		ieToggleFormElements();
	}

	$('#modalDimmer').hide();
	$('#modalPopup2').hide();
	$('#modalPopup2').draggable('destroy');

	popUpCallBack = null;
}

// Main function to display the pop up box
// strMessage   -   Message text to be displayed
// type         -   Type of message box to display
//              -   0  OK  Only
//              -   1  Yes No
//              -   2  Yes No Cancel
// callBack     -   Function to call with response
// buttontext   -   Text to be displayed on the button
// isCrmPop     -   True for CRM popup, False for normal one
// showDimmer   -   Flag whether to show the dimmer before the popup, or not (true/false)
//
// Returns :-
//              - -1 [Cancel]
//              -  0 [No]
//              -  1 [Yes]
//
function showPopUp (strMessage, type, callBack, buttontext, isCrmPop, showDimmer) {

	if ( typeof showDimmer == 'undefined' ) {
		showDimmer = true;
	}

	//. If the message is not null then update the dialog text
	if (strMessage != null) {
		$('#popText').html(strMessage);
	}

	// Assign the call back function to the global popUpCallBack var
	if (callBack != null) {
		popUpCallBack = callBack;
	}

	if (type == null) {
		// Default to a yes/no box
		type = 0;
	}

	// Currently we do yes/no and ok
	switch(type) {
		case 1:
			setupYesNo();
		break;
		case 2:
			setupOK(buttontext);
		break;
		case 3:
			setupYesNoCancel();
		case 4:
			setupOKCancel(buttontext);
		break;
		case 4:
			setupNoBtn();
		break;
		default:
			setupOK(buttontext);
	}

	if (isInetExpSix) {
		ieToggleFormElements();
	}
	
	// Show the dimmer before the popup
	if (showDimmer) {
		$('#modalDimmer').show();
	}

	if (isCrmPop) {
		$('#modalPopup2').css('width','595px');
		$('#modalPopup2').css('height','600px');
		$('#popupMain').css('background-image','url(http://whdn.williamhill.com/core/ob/static/cust/images/en/popupCrmBG.png)');
		$('#popupTop').css('background-image','url(http://whdn.williamhill.com/core/ob/static/cust/images/en/popupCrmTop.png)');
	}
	else {
		$('#modalPopup2').css('width','326px');
		$('#modalPopup2').css('height','80px');
		$('#popupMain').css('background-image','url(http://whdn.williamhill.com/core/ob/static/cust/images/en/popupBG.png)');
		$('#popupTop').css('background-image','url(http://whdn.williamhill.com/core/ob/static/cust/images/en/popupTop.png)');
	}

	$('#modalPopup2').center();
	$('#modalPopup2').draggable({ containment: 'parent' });
	$('#modalPopup2').show();

}

function ieToggleFormElements () {
	$(':input').toggle();
}

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function remember_oi_overlay(remember,name) {
		var rem = (remember === true ? 1 : 0);
		document.site.set_pref(name,rem,null,0);
	}

	function build_oi_overlay(canvas_name, outer_id, closer_id, shade_id) {
		var url = document.ssl_ajax_url + '?action=GetCanvas&amp;canvas_name=' + canvas_name;

		HttpRequest(url,'GET',function cb(req) {

			var content = req.responseText;

			if (content == '') {
				printfire('Content is empty');
				return
			} else if (content.indexOf('OB_ERR_CMS_NOCANVAS') != -1) {
				printfire('The canvas(es) provided does not exist');
				return
			} else if (content.indexOf(outer_id) == -1 || content.indexOf(closer_id) == -1) {
				// the IDs SHOULD be in the canvas, but just incase...
				printfire('One or more of the given IDs does not exist in the loaded canvases');
				return
			}

			// add response to OIOverlayDiv
			$('#OIOverlayDiv').append(content);

			overlay = new SimpleOverlay(outer_id, shade_id, closer_id);
			overlay.show();

		},null,true);
	}
</script>

	
	
		<script type="text/javascript">
			function device_overlay() {
	
				if(display_MoD()) {
					// don't show DoM overlay if the customer has just logged out
					if (document.site.get_pref('dom_dsa') == 0 &amp;&amp; !getCookie(document.cust_logout_cookie_name)) {
						build_oi_overlay('DoMOverlay','DoMContainer','MoDDesktopOption','overlayShadeDiv');
					}
				}
			}
	
			function display_MoD() {
	
				var userNavigator = navigator.userAgent;
				var pattern = /iPad|iPhone|Android/g;
				var matchNavigator = pattern.test(userNavigator);
	
				return matchNavigator &amp;&amp; (typeof window.MSStream === 'undefined');
	
			}
	
			document.bodyOnLoad.push(device_overlay);
	
		</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

	var odds_display = 'ODDS';

	function filter_sport() {
		var f = document.forms['in_running'];
		f.submit();
	}

	document.ip_list = new LiveServEventList(
		'TYPE',
		'MKT_GRP'
	);

		document.ls_event_lists[document.ls_event_lists.length] = "ip_list";


</script>
	
	

<script type="text/javascript">

	document.uc_list = new LiveServEventList(
		'TYPE_UPCOMING',
		'MKT_GRP'
	);

	document.ls_event_lists[document.ls_event_lists.length] = "uc_list";

	document.uc_list.use_primary_mkts = false;
	document.uc_list.set_callback(overridden_ev_status_uc, 'ev_status_changed');

	document.ip_list.register_isoff('T', '295');
	document.bodyOnLoad.push(override_handlers);

	function override_handlers() {

		// Change the BIR handler for the event list
		// so that we can check if we need to remove
		// the newly started event from the upcoming matches list
		document.ip_list.bir.set_callback(is_off_handler, 'ISOFF');
		document.ip_list.bir.set_callback(is_about_to_start, 'ISSTARTING');
	}

	function is_about_to_start(_event) {
		change_highlights(_event);
		// Call the original handler to do the main work
		document.ip_list.is_about_to_start(_event);
		cleanup_highlights();
	}

	function is_off_handler(_event) {
		change_highlights(_event);
		// Call the original handler to do the main work
		document.ip_list.is_off_handler(_event);
		cleanup_highlights();
	}

	function change_highlights(_event) {

		if (_event.ev_has_bir == 'N') {
			/* We don't have a bir market, so ignore the event*/
			printfire('Cancel GoAjaxEvent request for ev_id: ' + _event.ev_id);
			return;
		}

		var _ev_id = _event.ev_id;

		printfire('Event ' + _ev_id + ' is off , primary market is ' + _event.ev_mkt_id);

		// Search the event on the upcoming matches list
		var e = document.uc_list.get_event(_ev_id);

		if (e != null) {
			// Remove the event from the upcoming matches list
			document.uc_list.delete_event(_ev_id);
			document.uc_list.remove_event_html(e,true);
		}
	}

	function overridden_ev_status_uc(event) {

		printfire ('Event (UC)' + event.ev_id + ' status is '+ event.status);

		var e = document.uc_list.get_event(event.ev_id);

		if(event.status == 'S' &amp;&amp; e != null){
			printfire('Removing (UC)' + event.ev_id);
			// Remove event
			document.uc_list.delete_event(event.ev_id);
			document.uc_list.remove_event_html(e,true);
		}
	}

</script>

	<link href="http://whdn.williamhill.com/core/ob/static/cust/css/en/topXBets.css?ver=86da42e8ca52528ce2660fd0b2e666af" type="text/css" rel="stylesheet" />


<script type="text/javascript" language="Javascript">



$(function() {
		$("#slider").slider({
			value:16,
			min: 1,
			max:52,
			step:1,
			slide: function(event, ui) {

				//calculate actual amount from slider value
				var stake, winnings;
				if (ui.value &lt; 10) {
					stake = (ui.value / 10);
				} else if (ui.value &lt; 30) {
					stake = 1 + (ui.value - 10);
				} else if (ui.value &lt; 46) {
					stake = 20 + ((ui.value - 30) * 5);
				} else {
					stake = 100 + ((ui.value - 46) * 25);
				}

				stake = stake.toFixed(2);
				winnings = stake * $("#rate").attr("value");

				$("#topxamountval").val(stake);
				$("#topxamount").val(' ' + stake);
				$("#topxprice").val(' '+ winnings.toFixed(2));
			}
		});
		$("#topxamountval").val('10.00');
		$("#topxamount").val(' ' + '10.00');
		$("#topxprice").val(' ' + (10.00 * $("#rate").attr("value")).toFixed(2));
});





var has_topx_bets = false;

function topXBetslipCheck() {
	has_topx_bets = document.betslip.have_bets();
}



function submitTopX() {

	if (has_topx_bets == false) {
		var accum_text = '';
		var topx_num = 6;
		var stake = document.getElementById("topxamountval").value;

		if (topx_num == 1) {
			accum_text = "L";
		} else if (topx_num == 2) {
			accum_text = "DBL";
		} else if (topx_num == 3) {
			accum_text = "TBL";
		} else if (topx_num == 4) {
			accum_text = "ACC4";
		} else if (topx_num == 5) {
			accum_text = "ACC5";
		} else if (topx_num == 6) {
			accum_text = "ACC6";
		} else if (topx_num == 7) {
			accum_text = "ACC7";
		}

		if (topx_num == 1) {
			var bs_field_id = "slip_sgl_stake";
		} else {
			var bs_field_id = "slip_combi_stake";
		}

		var bs_field_id = bs_field_id.concat(accum_text);

		var e = document.getElementById(bs_field_id);

		if (e != undefined) {
			e.value = stake;
			if (topx_num == 1) {
				document.betslip.single_stake_onblur(e, accum_text);
			} else {
				document.betslip.combi_stake_onblur(e, accum_text);
			}
			if (!document.betslip.is_push_enabled()) {
				document.betslip.check_bet_onclick();
			}
		}

	}
}


initTopX = function() {

	bgsleight.init();

	
		&lt;!-- expand to show the bets --&gt;
		toggle_topx_visibility('pricesblock');
	
}


function toggle_topx_visibility(id) {

	var e = document.getElementById(id);

	if(e.style.display == 'block') {
		 e.style.display = 'none';
		 addClass(document.getElementById('topxhidebetslink'), 'displayNone');
		 removeClass(document.getElementById('topxshowbetslink'), 'displayNone');

	} else {
		 e.style.display = 'block';
		 removeClass(document.getElementById('topxhidebetslink'), 'displayNone');
		 addClass(document.getElementById('topxshowbetslink'), 'displayNone');

	}
}



function trackTopX() {
	try {
		
	} catch (err) {
			printfire('Tracking tag error');
	}
}

document.bodyOnLoad.push(initTopX);

</script>

// Unica import mm cookie test

var passMMCk = '';

function readMMCk(mmCkName) {

        var rMMCk = "" + document.cookie;
        var ind = rMMCk.indexOf(mmCkName);
        if (ind == -1 || mmCkName == "") return ""; 
        var ind1 = rMMCk.indexOf(';', ind);
        if (ind1 == -1) ind1 = rMMCk.length; 
        var mmCKvalue = unescape(rMMCk.substring(ind + mmCkName.length +1, ind1));

                passMMCktemp = mmCkName+"="+mmCKvalue+"&amp;";
                passMMCk += passMMCktemp.replace("%2C", "-");

// window.alert('test' +passMMCk);
}
var isLiveTV = document.getElementById("liveTV");
                if (isLiveTV) {
readMMCk('UnicaNIODID');
isLiveTV.href = "javascript:window.open('http://www.williamhill.com/live-tv/?un=&amp;"+passMMCk+"','LiveTV','width=550,height=325');void(0);";
}

var mmCkMain = new Array('mmcore.mxLRvar','mmcore.mm_var','IBSMYMKTS','tmvt','vars_info','banner_click');

for( i=0; mmCkMain.length &gt; i; i++){
                readMMCk(mmCkMain[i]);
}
//window.alert(passMMCk);
NTPT_PGEXTRA += '&amp;'+passMMCk;
//window.alert(passMMCk);
//window.alert(NTPT_PGEXTRA);

        }
}

function getURLParameter(name) {
    return decodeURI(
        (RegExp(name + '=' + '(.+?)(&amp;|$)').exec(location.search)||[,null])[1]
    );
}

var trafalgarVerticalChoice = 'tennis';

function displayTrafalgarOverlay(option) {
    document.getElementById('trafalgarOverlayShadeDiv').style.display = 'block';
    document.getElementById('trafalgarABTestOverlay').style.display = 'block';
    trafalgarVerticalChoice = option;
}
function processTrafalgarNavigation(goToTrafalgar) {
    var trafalgarOrNotUrl = '/bet/en-gb/betting/y/17/Tennis.html';
    var intcidValue = '?intcid=trafalgar-TennisBetaNo';

    if (trafalgarVerticalChoice === 'golf') {
        trafalgarOrNotUrl = '/bet/en-gb/betting/y/6/Golf.html';
        intcidValue = '?intcid=trafalgar-GolfBetaNo';
    }
    
    if (setCookie &amp;&amp; document.pref_cookie_path &amp;&amp; document.pref_cookie_domain) {
      if (goToTrafalgar) {
        var expiryDate = new Date('January 08, 3000');
        setCookie('wh_traf_public_beta', 'Yes', expiryDate, document.pref_cookie_path, document.pref_cookie_domain, ''); 
        intcidValue = '?intcid=trafalgar-TennisBetaYes';
        if (trafalgarVerticalChoice === 'golf') {
          intcidValue = '?intcid=trafalgar-GolfBetaYes';
        }
      }
      else {
        if (window.sessionStorage) {
          window.sessionStorage.setItem('trafalgarDeclined', 'true');
        }
      }
    }
    trafalgarOrNotUrl = trafalgarOrNotUrl + intcidValue;
    window.location.href = trafalgarOrNotUrl;
}

function getURLParameter(name) {
    return decodeURI(
        (RegExp(name + '=' + '(.+?)(&amp;|$)').exec(location.search)||[,null])[1]
    );
}
